Let me first verify correctness of a few answers by computing them:

**Q11 - Rec_function(6):**
- Rec_function(6): 6 is even → 6 * Rec_function(4)
- Rec_function(4): 4 is even → 4 * Rec_function(2)
- Rec_function(2): 2 is even → 2 * Rec_function(0)
- Rec_function(0): return 1
- So: 2*1=2, 4*2=8, 6*8=48 ✓ Answer is (e) 48

**Q7 - Time complexity:** The code has a for loop O(f²) and a while loop O(f²). Total O(f²). ✓ Answer is (b) O(f²)
